14:05 < kiwi0530> TaipeiWar: Michael_Wu接著要帶去的是耐踩圓線，我在想應該是多芯的同軸電纜
14:05 < TaipeiWar> Here's the 10 second rundown of how to review things on Transifex, for those with reviewer status:
14:05 < TaipeiWar> •From the language team page, click on r2.pot, then "Translate Now"
14:05 < TaipeiWar> •From there, uncheck the boxes for "Remaining" and "Reviewed" (leaving just "Translated" strings as your 'queue' of things to work on)
14:05 < TaipeiWar> •As you check out each source string and matching translation, if it looks good, check the box on the rightmost column to mark it as reviewed. If it needs work, you can either edit it directly, or leave a suggestion for someone else to look at (with how the Transifex UI works, I'd recommend the former - you can also just skip them initially and get
14:05 < TaipeiWar>  back to them later).
14:05 < TaipeiWar> Final note: Don't feel as if you need to get through all of it. There are no deadlines. Anything you get to is great, and anything else can get sorted out later.
